		<div class="flex absolute bottom-5 left-1/2 z-30 -translate-x-1/2 items-center gap-2">
			<button type="button" class="rounded-full shadow-lg" aria-label="Anterior" data-l7-prev>

		<a class="inline-flex w-full items-center justify-between text-end" href="/ultima-hora" target="_parent"><span class="w-full pr-1">Ver más</span> <svg fill="#000000" class="w-4 h-4" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 640 640"><path d="M297.4 438.6C309.9 451.1 330.2 451.1 342.7 438.6L502.7 278.6C515.2 266.1 515.2 245.8 502.7 233.3C490.2 220.8 469.9 220.8 457.4 233.3L320 370.7L182.6 233.4C170.1 220.9 149.8 220.9 137.3 233.4C124.8 245.9 124.8 266.2 137.3 278.7L297.3 438.7z"/></svg>
		</a>

	<script>
	(function() {
		const root = document.getElementById('default-carousel-1530');
		if (!root) return;
		const items = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-item]'));
		const viewport = root.querySelector('[data-l7-viewport]');
		const prev = root.querySelector('[data-l7-prev]');
		const next = root.querySelector('[data-l7-next]');
		if (!items.length) return;

		let index = 0;

		const transitionMs = 1200;
		const intervalMs = 12500;
		let timer = null;
		let animating = false;
		let showToken = 0;
		const setViewportHeight = (item) => {
			if (!viewport || !item) return;
			const h = item.offsetHeight;
			if (h > 0) {
				viewport.style.height = h + 'px';
			} else {
				viewport.style.removeProperty('height');
			}
		};

		const show = (nextIndex, direction = 1) => {
			const total = items.length;
			const safe = ((nextIndex % total) + total) % total;
			showToken += 1;
			const token = showToken;
			animating = true;
			if (safe === index) {
				animating = false;
				return;
			}
			const current = items[index];
			const nextItem = items[safe];
			const dir = direction >= 0 ? 1 : -1;
			nextItem.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
			nextItem.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
			setViewportHeight(nextItem);
			requestAnimationFrame(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? '-translate-x-full' : 'translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			});
			setTimeout(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.add('hidden');
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove('translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
				index = safe;
				animating = false;
			}, transitionMs);
		};

		const stop = () => {
			if (!timer) return;
			clearTimeout(timer);
			timer = null;
		};
		const schedule = () => {
			stop();
			timer = setTimeout(() => go(1, { force: true }), intervalMs);
		};
		const go = (stepOrIndex, options = {}) => {
			const { absolute = false, force = false } = options;
			if (animating && !force) return;
			const nextIndex = absolute ? stepOrIndex : index + stepOrIndex;
			const direction = absolute ? (nextIndex > index ? 1 : -1) : stepOrIndex;
			show(nextIndex, direction);
			schedule();
		};

		items.forEach((item, i) => {
			if (i === index) {
				item.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			} else {
				item.classList.add('hidden');
				item.classList.remove('translate-x-0', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-full');
			}
		});
		setViewportHeight(items[index]);
		schedule();

		if (prev) {
			prev.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(-1);
			});
		}
		if (next) {
			next.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(1);
			});
		}

		let startX = 0;
		let startY = 0;
		let tracking = false;

		root.addEventListener('touchstart', (event) => {
			if (event.target && event.target.closest && event.target.closest('[data-l7-slide-to]')) {
				tracking = false;
				return;
			}
			if (!event.touches || event.touches.length !== 1) return;
			tracking = true;
			const touch = event.touches[0];
			startX = touch.clientX;
			startY = touch.clientY;
			stop();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchend', (event) => {
			if (!tracking) return;
			tracking = false;
			const touch = event.changedTouches && event.changedTouches[0];
			if (!touch) {
				schedule();
				return;
			}
			const dx = touch.clientX - startX;
			const dy = touch.clientY - startY;
			if (Math.abs(dx) > 40 && Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
				go(dx < 0 ? 1 : -1);
				return;
			}
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchcancel', () => {
			tracking = false;
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });

		window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
			setViewportHeight(items[index]);
		});
	})();
	</script>

</div>

en Ecuador</a></h1><div class="story-publishup afacad-flux font-light uppercase text-sm text-[#929497]" itemprop="datePublished">23 de Febrero de 2026</div></div></article></div><div class="flex font-normal text-base leading-[1.35rem]" itemprop="name"><a href="/noticias/nacionales/210/cal-sanciona-a-dos-asambleistas-del-correismo-por-faltas-muy-graves" itemprop="url">CAL sanciona a dos asamble&iacute;stas del corre&iacute;smo por faltas &#039;muy graves&#039;</a></h1><div class="story-publishup afacad-flux font-light uppercase text-sm text-[#929497]" itemprop="datePublished">23 de         <!-- Slider indicators -->
        <div class="flex absolute bottom-3 left-1/2 z-30 -translate-x-1/2 items-center gap-1">
			<button type="button" class="rounded-full shadow-lg" aria-label="Anterior" data-l7-prev>
				<img class="h-6 w-6" src="https://www.eltelegrafo.com.ec/images/sitio/arrow-left.svg" alt="Anterior">
			</button>
        	<button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="true" aria-label="Slide 1" data-l7-slide-to="0"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 2" data-l7-slide-to="1"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 3" data-l7-slide-to="2"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 4" data-l7-slide-to="3"></button>			<button type="button" class="rounded-full shadow-lg" aria-label="Siguiente" data-l7-next>
				<img class="h-6 w-6" src="https://www.eltelegrafo.com.ec/images/sitio/arrow-right.svg" alt="Siguiente">
			</button>
        </div>
	</div>

	<script>
	(function() {
		const root = document.getElementById('default-carousel-1573');
		if (!root) return;
		const items = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-item]'));
		const dots = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-slide-to]'));
		const prev = root.querySelector('[data-l7-prev]');
		const next = root.querySelector('[data-l7-next]');
		if (!items.length) return;

		let index = dots.findIndex((dot) => dot.getAttribute('aria-current') === 'true');
		if (index < 0) index = 0;

		const transitionMs = 1200;
		const intervalMs = 15000;
		let timer = null;
		let animating = false;
		let showToken = 0;
		const updateDots = (activeIndex) => {
			dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
				const isActive = i === activeIndex;
				dot.setAttribute('aria-current', isActive ? 'true' : 'false');
				if (isActive) {
					dot.classList.remove('dot-animate');
					void dot.offsetWidth;
					dot.classList.add('dot-animate');
				}
			});
		};

		const show = (nextIndex, direction = 1) => {
			const total = items.length;
			const safe = ((nextIndex % total) + total) % total;
			showToken += 1;
			const token = showToken;
			animating = true;
			if (safe === index) {
				updateDots(safe);
				animating = false;
				return;
			}
			const current = items[index];
			const nextItem = items[safe];
			const dir = direction >= 0 ? 1 : -1;
			nextItem.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
			nextItem.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
			requestAnimationFrame(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? '-translate-x-full' : 'translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			});
			updateDots(safe);
			setTimeout(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.add('hidden');
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove('translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
				index = safe;
				animating = false;
			}, transitionMs);
		};

		const stop = () => {
			if (!timer) return;
			clearTimeout(timer);
			timer = null;
		};
		const schedule = () => {
			stop();
			timer = setTimeout(() => go(1, { force: true }), intervalMs);
		};
		const go = (stepOrIndex, options = {}) => {
			const { absolute = false, force = false } = options;
			if (animating && !force) return;
			const nextIndex = absolute ? stepOrIndex : index + stepOrIndex;
			const direction = absolute ? (nextIndex > index ? 1 : -1) : stepOrIndex;
			show(nextIndex, direction);
			schedule();
		};

		items.forEach((item, i) => {
			if (i === index) {
				item.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			} else {
				item.classList.add('hidden');
				item.classList.remove('translate-x-0', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-full');
			}
		});
		updateDots(index);
		schedule();

		if (prev) {
			prev.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(-1);
			});
		}
		if (next) {
			next.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(1);
			});
		}

		dots.forEach((dot) => {
			dot.addEventListener('click', () => {
				const nextIndex = Number(dot.getAttribute('data-l7-slide-to') || 0);
				go(nextIndex, { absolute: true });
			});
		});

		let startX = 0;
		let startY = 0;
		let tracking = false;

		root.addEventListener('touchstart', (event) => {
			if (event.target && event.target.closest && event.target.closest('[data-l7-slide-to]')) {
				tracking = false;
				return;
			}
			if (!event.touches || event.touches.length !== 1) return;
			tracking = true;
			const touch = event.touches[0];
			startX = touch.clientX;
			startY = touch.clientY;
			stop();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchend', (event) => {
			if (!tracking) return;
			tracking = false;
			const touch = event.changedTouches && event.changedTouches[0];
			if (!touch) {
				schedule();
				return;
			}
			const dx = touch.clientX - startX;
			const dy = touch.clientY - startY;
			if (Math.abs(dx) > 40 && Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
				go(dx < 0 ? 1 : -1);
				return;
			}
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchcancel', () => {
			tracking = false;
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });
	})();
	</script>

	
</div>

  <path d="M4.19.01C.71.21-1.21,4.21.84,7.06c1.99,2.77,6.26,2.35,7.67-.75C9.9,3.25,7.53-.18,4.19.01ZM7.07,5.26H1.85v-1.61h5.22v1.61Z"/></svg></a></div></div></div><div class="addon-module py-1 hidden md:block"><div id="mod-1533" class="s-layout-2 s-mod style-006db3 ">

						<article class="item s" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
							<div class="story-introtext afacad-flux font-light text-right" itemprop="description">
								<span class="story-heading afacad-flux font-extrabold text-right" itemprop="name">

		<div class="flex absolute bottom-5 left-1/2 z-30 -translate-x-1/2 items-center gap-2">
			<button type="button" class="rounded-full shadow-lg" aria-label="Anterior" data-l7-prev>
				<img class="h-6 w-6" src="https://www.eltelegrafo.com.ec/images/sitio/arrow-left.svg" alt="Anterior">
			</button>
			<button type="button" class="rounded-full shadow-lg" aria-label="Siguiente" data-l7-next>
				<img class="h-6 w-6" src="https://www.eltelegrafo.com.ec/images/sitio/arrow-right.svg" alt="Siguiente">
			</button>
		</div>

	<script>
	(function() {
		const root = document.getElementById('default-carousel-1533');
		if (!root) return;
		const items = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-item]'));
		const viewport = root.querySelector('[data-l7-viewport]');
		const prev = root.querySelector('[data-l7-prev]');
		const next = root.querySelector('[data-l7-next]');
		if (!items.length) return;

		let index = 0;

		const transitionMs = 1200;
		const intervalMs = 12500;
		let timer = null;
		let animating = false;
		let showToken = 0;
		const setViewportHeight = (item) => {
			if (!viewport || !item) return;
			const h = item.offsetHeight;
			if (h > 0) {
				viewport.style.height = h + 'px';
			} else {
				viewport.style.removeProperty('height');
			}
		};

		const show = (nextIndex, direction = 1) => {
			const total = items.length;
			const safe = ((nextIndex % total) + total) % total;
			showToken += 1;
			const token = showToken;
			animating = true;
			if (safe === index) {
				animating = false;
				return;
			}
			const current = items[index];
			const nextItem = items[safe];
			const dir = direction >= 0 ? 1 : -1;
			nextItem.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
			nextItem.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
			setViewportHeight(nextItem);
			requestAnimationFrame(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? '-translate-x-full' : 'translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			});
			setTimeout(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.add('hidden');
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove('translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
				index = safe;
				animating = false;
			}, transitionMs);
		};

		const stop = () => {
			if (!timer) return;
			clearTimeout(timer);
			timer = null;
		};
		const schedule = () => {
			stop();
			timer = setTimeout(() => go(1, { force: true }), intervalMs);
		};
		const go = (stepOrIndex, options = {}) => {
			const { absolute = false, force = false } = options;
			if (animating && !force) return;
			const nextIndex = absolute ? stepOrIndex : index + stepOrIndex;
			const direction = absolute ? (nextIndex > index ? 1 : -1) : stepOrIndex;
			show(nextIndex, direction);
			schedule();
		};

		items.forEach((item, i) => {
			if (i === index) {
				item.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			} else {
				item.classList.add('hidden');
				item.classList.remove('translate-x-0', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-full');
			}
		});
		setViewportHeight(items[index]);
		schedule();

		if (prev) {
			prev.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(-1);
			});
		}
		if (next) {
			next.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(1);
			});
		}

		let startX = 0;
		let startY = 0;
		let tracking = false;

		root.addEventListener('touchstart', (event) => {
			if (event.target && event.target.closest && event.target.closest('[data-l7-slide-to]')) {
				tracking = false;
				return;
			}
			if (!event.touches || event.touches.length !== 1) return;
			tracking = true;
			const touch = event.touches[0];
			startX = touch.clientX;
			startY = touch.clientY;
			stop();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchend', (event) => {
			if (!tracking) return;
			tracking = false;
			const touch = event.changedTouches && event.changedTouches[0];
			if (!touch) {
				schedule();
				return;
			}
			const dx = touch.clientX - startX;
			const dy = touch.clientY - startY;
			if (Math.abs(dx) > 40 && Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
				go(dx < 0 ? 1 : -1);
				return;
			}
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchcancel', () => {
			tracking = false;
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });

		window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
			setViewportHeight(items[index]);
		});
	})();
	</script>

</div>

	<script data-cfasync="false" src="/cdn-cgi/scripts/5c5dd728/cloudflare-static/email-decode.min.js"></script><script>
	(function() {
		const root = document.getElementById('default-carousel-1603');
		if (!root) return;
		const items = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-item]'));
		const viewport = root.querySelector('[data-l7-viewport]');
		const prev = root.querySelector('[data-l7-prev]');
		const next = root.querySelector('[data-l7-next]');
		if (!items.length) return;

		let index = 0;

		const transitionMs = 1200;
		const intervalMs = 12500;
		let timer = null;
		let animating = false;
		let showToken = 0;
		const setViewportHeight = (item) => {
			if (!viewport || !item) return;
			const h = item.offsetHeight;
			if (h > 0) {
				viewport.style.height = h + 'px';
			} else {
				viewport.style.removeProperty('height');
			}
		};

		const show = (nextIndex, direction = 1) => {
			const total = items.length;
			const safe = ((nextIndex % total) + total) % total;
			showToken += 1;
			const token = showToken;
			animating = true;
			if (safe === index) {
				animating = false;
				return;
			}
			const current = items[index];
			const nextItem = items[safe];
			const dir = direction >= 0 ? 1 : -1;
			nextItem.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
			nextItem.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
			setViewportHeight(nextItem);
			requestAnimationFrame(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? '-translate-x-full' : 'translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			});
			setTimeout(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.add('hidden');
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove('translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
				index = safe;
				animating = false;
			}, transitionMs);
		};

		const stop = () => {
			if (!timer) return;
			clearTimeout(timer);
			timer = null;
		};
		const schedule = () => {
			stop();
			timer = setTimeout(() => go(1, { force: true }), intervalMs);
		};
		const go = (stepOrIndex, options = {}) => {
			const { absolute = false, force = false } = options;
			if (animating && !force) return;
			const nextIndex = absolute ? stepOrIndex : index + stepOrIndex;
			const direction = absolute ? (nextIndex > index ? 1 : -1) : stepOrIndex;
			show(nextIndex, direction);
			schedule();
		};

		items.forEach((item, i) => {
			if (i === index) {
				item.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			} else {
				item.classList.add('hidden');
				item.classList.remove('translate-x-0', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-full');
			}
		});
		setViewportHeight(items[index]);
		schedule();

		if (prev) {
			prev.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(-1);
			});
		}
		if (next) {
			next.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(1);
			});
		}

		let startX = 0;
		let startY = 0;
		let tracking = false;

		root.addEventListener('touchstart', (event) => {
			if (event.target && event.target.closest && event.target.closest('[data-l7-slide-to]')) {
				tracking = false;
				return;
			}
			if (!event.touches || event.touches.length !== 1) return;
			tracking = true;
			const touch = event.touches[0];
			startX = touch.clientX;
			startY = touch.clientY;
			stop();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchend', (event) => {
			if (!tracking) return;
			tracking = false;
			const touch = event.changedTouches && event.changedTouches[0];
			if (!touch) {
				schedule();
				return;
			}
			const dx = touch.clientX - startX;
			const dy = touch.clientY - startY;
			if (Math.abs(dx) > 40 && Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
				go(dx < 0 ? 1 : -1);
				return;
			}
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchcancel', () => {
			tracking = false;
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });

		window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
			setViewportHeight(items[index]);
		});
	})();
	</script>

</div>

												Ecuador entre los favoritos del Atl&eacute;tico de Madrid					</a>

        	<button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="true" aria-label="Slide 1" data-l7-slide-to="0"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 2" data-l7-slide-to="1"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 3" data-l7-slide-to="2"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 4" data-l7-slide-to="3"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 5" data-l7-slide-to="4"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 6" data-l7-slide-to="5"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 7" data-l7-slide-to="6"></button>			<button type="button" class=" rounded-full shadow-lg" aria-label="Siguiente" data-l7-next>
				<img class="h-6 w-6" src="https://www.eltelegrafo.com.ec/images/sitio/arrow-right.svg" alt="Siguiente">
			</button>
        </div>
	</div>

	<script>
	(function() {
		const root = document.getElementById('default-carousel-1550');
		if (!root) return;
		const items = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-item]'));
		const dots = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-slide-to]'));
		const prev = root.querySelector('[data-l7-prev]');
		const next = root.querySelector('[data-l7-next]');
		if (!items.length) return;

		let index = dots.findIndex((dot) => dot.getAttribute('aria-current') === 'true');
		if (index < 0) index = 0;

		const transitionMs = 1200;
		const intervalMs = 15000;
		let timer = null;
		let animating = false;
		let showToken = 0;
		const updateDots = (activeIndex) => {
			dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
				const isActive = i === activeIndex;
				dot.setAttribute('aria-current', isActive ? 'true' : 'false');
				if (isActive) {
					dot.classList.remove('dot-animate');
					void dot.offsetWidth;
					dot.classList.add('dot-animate');
				}
			});
		};

		const show = (next, direction = 1) => {
			const total = items.length;
			const safe = ((next % total) + total) % total;
			showToken += 1;
			const token = showToken;
			animating = true;
			if (safe === index) {
				updateDots(safe);
				animating = false;
				return;
			}
			const current = items[index];
			const nextItem = items[safe];
			const dir = direction >= 0 ? 1 : -1;
			nextItem.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
			nextItem.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
			requestAnimationFrame(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? '-translate-x-full' : 'translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			});
			updateDots(safe);
			setTimeout(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.add('hidden');
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove('translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
				index = safe;
				animating = false;
			}, transitionMs);
		};

		const stop = () => {
			if (!timer) return;
			clearTimeout(timer);
			timer = null;
		};
		const schedule = () => {
			stop();
			timer = setTimeout(() => go(1, { force: true }), intervalMs);
		};
		const go = (stepOrIndex, options = {}) => {
			const { absolute = false, force = false } = options;
			if (animating && !force) return;
			const next = absolute ? stepOrIndex : index + stepOrIndex;
			const direction = absolute ? (next > index ? 1 : -1) : stepOrIndex;
			show(next, direction);
			schedule();
		};

		items.forEach((item, i) => {
			if (i === index) {
				item.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			} else {
				item.classList.add('hidden');
				item.classList.remove('translate-x-0', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-full');
			}
		});
		updateDots(index);
		schedule();

		if (prev) {
			prev.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(-1);
			});
		}
		if (next) {
			next.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(1);
			});
		}

		dots.forEach((dot) => {
			dot.addEventListener('click', () => {
				const next = Number(dot.getAttribute('data-l7-slide-to') || 0);
				go(next, { absolute: true });
			});
		});

		let startX = 0;
		let startY = 0;
		let tracking = false;

		root.addEventListener('touchstart', (event) => {
			if (event.target && event.target.closest && event.target.closest('[data-l7-slide-to]')) {
				tracking = false;
				return;
			}
			if (!event.touches || event.touches.length !== 1) return;
			tracking = true;
			const touch = event.touches[0];
			startX = touch.clientX;
			startY = touch.clientY;
			stop();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchend', (event) => {
			if (!tracking) return;
			tracking = false;
			const touch = event.changedTouches && event.changedTouches[0];
			if (!touch) {
				schedule();
				return;
			}
			const dx = touch.clientX - startX;
			const dy = touch.clientY - startY;
			if (Math.abs(dx) > 40 && Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
				go(dx < 0 ? 1 : -1);
				return;
			}
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchcancel', () => {
			tracking = false;
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });
	})();
	</script>

	
</div>

				<img class="h-6 w-6" src="https://www.eltelegrafo.com.ec/images/sitio/arrow-right.svg" alt="Siguiente">
			</button>
        </div>
	</div>

	<script>
	(function() {
		const root = document.getElementById('default-carousel-1537');
		if (!root) return;
		const items = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-item]'));
		const dots = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-slide-to]'));
		const prev = root.querySelector('[data-l7-prev]');
		const next = root.querySelector('[data-l7-next]');
		if (!items.length) return;

		let index = dots.findIndex((dot) => dot.getAttribute('aria-current') === 'true');
		if (index < 0) index = 0;

		const transitionMs = 1200;
		const intervalMs = 15000;
		let timer = null;
		let animating = false;
		let showToken = 0;
		const updateDots = (activeIndex) => {
			dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
				const isActive = i === activeIndex;
				dot.setAttribute('aria-current', isActive ? 'true' : 'false');
				if (isActive) {
					dot.classList.remove('dot-animate');
					void dot.offsetWidth;
					dot.classList.add('dot-animate');
				}
			});
		};

		const show = (next, direction = 1) => {
			const total = items.length;
			const safe = ((next % total) + total) % total;
			showToken += 1;
			const token = showToken;
			animating = true;
			if (safe === index) {
				updateDots(safe);
				animating = false;
				return;
			}
			const current = items[index];
			const nextItem = items[safe];
			const dir = direction >= 0 ? 1 : -1;
			nextItem.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
			nextItem.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
			requestAnimationFrame(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? '-translate-x-full' : 'translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			});
			updateDots(safe);
			setTimeout(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.add('hidden');
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove('translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
				index = safe;
				animating = false;
			}, transitionMs);
		};

		const stop = () => {
			if (!timer) return;
			clearTimeout(timer);
			timer = null;
		};
		const schedule = () => {
			stop();
			timer = setTimeout(() => go(1, { force: true }), intervalMs);
		};
		const go = (stepOrIndex, options = {}) => {
			const { absolute = false, force = false } = options;
			if (animating && !force) return;
			const next = absolute ? stepOrIndex : index + stepOrIndex;
			const direction = absolute ? (next > index ? 1 : -1) : stepOrIndex;
			show(next, direction);
			schedule();
		};

		items.forEach((item, i) => {
			if (i === index) {
				item.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			} else {
				item.classList.add('hidden');
				item.classList.remove('translate-x-0', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-full');
			}
		});
		updateDots(index);
		schedule();

		if (prev) {
			prev.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(-1);
			});
		}
		if (next) {
			next.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(1);
			});
		}

		dots.forEach((dot) => {
			dot.addEventListener('click', () => {
				const next = Number(dot.getAttribute('data-l7-slide-to') || 0);
				go(next, { absolute: true });
			});
		});

		let startX = 0;
		let startY = 0;
		let tracking = false;

		root.addEventListener('touchstart', (event) => {
			if (event.target && event.target.closest && event.target.closest('[data-l7-slide-to]')) {
				tracking = false;
				return;
			}
			if (!event.touches || event.touches.length !== 1) return;
			tracking = true;
			const touch = event.touches[0];
			startX = touch.clientX;
			startY = touch.clientY;
			stop();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchend', (event) => {
			if (!tracking) return;
			tracking = false;
			const touch = event.changedTouches && event.changedTouches[0];
			if (!touch) {
				schedule();
				return;
			}
			const dx = touch.clientX - startX;
			const dy = touch.clientY - startY;
			if (Math.abs(dx) > 40 && Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
				go(dx < 0 ? 1 : -1);
				return;
			}
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchcancel', () => {
			tracking = false;
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });
	})();
	</script>

	
</div>
</div><div class="addon-bottom-multi flex justify-center items-center py-1">

					            <h1 class="story-heading afacad-flux font-normal md:font-light text-base md:text-lg leading-[1.35rem] pb-2" itemprop="name">
	                <a href="/noticias/tendencias/213/influencer-asustada-fantasma-transmision-en-vivo" itemprop="url">
												Influencer asustada por un fantasma en transmisi&oacute;n en vivo					</a>
	            </h1>
	            	            <div class="story-publishup afacad-flux font-light uppercase text-sm md:text-base text-[#929497]" itemprop="datePublished">23 de Febrero de 2026</div>
	            	            <div class="story-publishup afacad-flux font-light uppercase text-sm md:text-base text-[#929497]" itemprop="datePublished"></div>				
			</div>
		</article>
	</div>
								<div class="flex flex-wrap  md:pb-4 border-b-0 md:border-b-2 border-b-[#f8b804]">
		<article class="mx-auto w-full flex flex-wrap item p" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
			<div class="image basis-1/4 md:basis-full">
				<a class="story-image" href="/noticias/tendencias/213/mrbeast-construye-dos-escuelas-amazonia-ecuador">
					<picture class="lazyload" data-expand="-20" data-isvideo="1">
	                	<img class="max-w-full h-auto blur-up lazyload" src="/media/k2/items/cache/8bbb0b60f52d2d590fde4dd688de78ff_XL.jpg" data-src="/media/k2/items/cache/8bbb0b60f52d2d590fde4dd688de78ff_XL.jpg" alt="Ecuador aparece en el nuevo video de MrBeast con la entrega de dos escuelas en la selva" itemprop="image">
	            	</picture>
				</a>
			</div>

			<button type="button" class="rounded-full shadow-lg" aria-label="Anterior" data-l7-prev>
				<img class="h-6 w-6" src="https://www.eltelegrafo.com.ec/images/sitio/arrow-left.svg" alt="Anterior">

        	<button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="true" aria-label="Slide 2" data-l7-slide-to="0"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 3" data-l7-slide-to="1"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 4" data-l7-slide-to="2"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 5" data-l7-slide-to="3"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 6" data-l7-slide-to="4"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 7" data-l7-slide-to="5"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 8" data-l7-slide-to="6"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 9" data-l7-slide-to="7"></button>			<button type="button" class="rounded-full shadow-lg" aria-label="Siguiente" data-l7-next>

	<script>
	(function() {
		const root = document.getElementById('default-carousel-1543');
		if (!root) return;
		const items = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-item]'));
		const dots = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-slide-to]'));
		const prev = root.querySelector('[data-l7-prev]');
		const next = root.querySelector('[data-l7-next]');
		if (!items.length) return;

		let index = dots.findIndex((dot) => dot.getAttribute('aria-current') === 'true');
		if (index < 0) index = 0;

		const transitionMs = 1200;
		const intervalMs = 15000;
		let timer = null;
		let animating = false;
		let showToken = 0;
		const updateDots = (activeIndex) => {
			dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
				const isActive = i === activeIndex;
				dot.setAttribute('aria-current', isActive ? 'true' : 'false');
				if (isActive) {
					dot.classList.remove('dot-animate');
					void dot.offsetWidth;
					dot.classList.add('dot-animate');
				}
			});
		};

		const show = (nextIndex, direction = 1) => {
			const total = items.length;
			const safe = ((nextIndex % total) + total) % total;
			showToken += 1;
			const token = showToken;
			animating = true;
			if (safe === index) {
				updateDots(safe);
				animating = false;
				return;
			}
			const current = items[index];
			const nextItem = items[safe];
			const dir = direction >= 0 ? 1 : -1;
			nextItem.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
			nextItem.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
			requestAnimationFrame(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? '-translate-x-full' : 'translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			});
			updateDots(safe);
			setTimeout(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.add('hidden');
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove('translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
				index = safe;
				animating = false;
			}, transitionMs);
		};

		const stop = () => {
			if (!timer) return;
			clearTimeout(timer);
			timer = null;
		};
		const schedule = () => {
			stop();
			timer = setTimeout(() => go(1, { force: true }), intervalMs);
		};
		const go = (stepOrIndex, options = {}) => {
			const { absolute = false, force = false } = options;
			if (animating && !force) return;
			const nextIndex = absolute ? stepOrIndex : index + stepOrIndex;
			const direction = absolute ? (nextIndex > index ? 1 : -1) : stepOrIndex;
			show(nextIndex, direction);
			schedule();
		};

		items.forEach((item, i) => {
			if (i === index) {
				item.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			} else {
				item.classList.add('hidden');
				item.classList.remove('translate-x-0', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-full');
			}
		});
		updateDots(index);
		schedule();

		if (prev) {
			prev.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(-1);
			});
		}
		if (next) {
			next.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(1);
			});
		}

		dots.forEach((dot) => {
			dot.addEventListener('click', () => {
				const nextIndex = Number(dot.getAttribute('data-l7-slide-to') || 0);
				go(nextIndex, { absolute: true });
			});
		});

		let startX = 0;
		let startY = 0;
		let tracking = false;

		root.addEventListener('touchstart', (event) => {
			if (event.target && event.target.closest && event.target.closest('[data-l7-slide-to]')) {
				tracking = false;
				return;
			}
			if (!event.touches || event.touches.length !== 1) return;
			tracking = true;
			const touch = event.touches[0];
			startX = touch.clientX;
			startY = touch.clientY;
			stop();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchend', (event) => {
			if (!tracking) return;
			tracking = false;
			const touch = event.changedTouches && event.changedTouches[0];
			if (!touch) {
				schedule();
				return;
			}
			const dx = touch.clientX - startX;
			const dy = touch.clientY - startY;
			if (Math.abs(dx) > 40 && Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
				go(dx < 0 ? 1 : -1);
				return;
			}
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchcancel', () => {
			tracking = false;
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });
	})();
	</script>

	
</div>

font-light uppercase text-sm text-[#929497]" itemprop="datePublished">29 de Enero de 2026</div></div></article></div></div><div class="hidden absolute inset-0 transition-transform duration-1200 ease-in-out translate-x-full" data-l7-item><div class="flex flex-wrap"><article class="mx-auto w-full flex flex-wrap item s" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article"><div class="caption tropicales</a></h1><div class="story-publishup afacad-flux font-light uppercase text-sm text-[#929497]" itemprop="datePublished">23 de Enero de 2026</div></div></article></div></div><div class="hidden absolute inset-0 transition-transform duration-1200 ease-in-out translate-x-full" data-l7-item><div class="flex flex-wrap"><article class="mx-auto w-full flex flex-wrap item s" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article"><div class="caption basis-full pl-2"><h1 class="story-heading afacad-flux font-normal text-base leading-[1.35rem]" itemprop="name"><a href="/noticias/recetas/206/torta-de-pina-y-maduros" itemprop="url">Torta de pi&ntilde;a y maduros</a></h1><div class="story-publishup afacad-flux font-light uppercase text-sm text-[#929497]"         <div class="flex absolute bottom-5 left-1/2 z-30 -translate-x-1/2 items-center gap-1">
			<button type="button" class="rounded-full shadow-lg" aria-label="Anterior" data-l7-prev>
				<img class="h-6 w-6" src="https://www.eltelegrafo.com.ec/images/sitio/arrow-left.svg" alt="Anterior">
			</button>
        	<button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="true" aria-label="Slide 2" data-l7-slide-to="0"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 3" data-l7-slide-to="1"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 4" data-l7-slide-to="2"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 5" data-l7-slide-to="3"></button>			<button type="button" class="rounded-full shadow-lg" aria-label="Siguiente" data-l7-next>
				<img class="h-6 w-6" src="https://www.eltelegrafo.com.ec/images/sitio/arrow-right.svg" alt="Siguiente">
			</button>

	<script>
	(function() {
		const root = document.getElementById('default-carousel-1549');
		if (!root) return;
		const items = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-item]'));
		const dots = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-slide-to]'));
		const prev = root.querySelector('[data-l7-prev]');
		const next = root.querySelector('[data-l7-next]');
		if (!items.length) return;

		let index = dots.findIndex((dot) => dot.getAttribute('aria-current') === 'true');
		if (index < 0) index = 0;

		const transitionMs = 1200;
		const intervalMs = 15000;
		let timer = null;
		let animating = false;
		let showToken = 0;
		const updateDots = (activeIndex) => {
			dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
				const isActive = i === activeIndex;
				dot.setAttribute('aria-current', isActive ? 'true' : 'false');
				if (isActive) {
					dot.classList.remove('dot-animate');
					void dot.offsetWidth;
					dot.classList.add('dot-animate');
				}
			});
		};

		const show = (nextIndex, direction = 1) => {
			const total = items.length;
			const safe = ((nextIndex % total) + total) % total;
			showToken += 1;
			const token = showToken;
			animating = true;
			if (safe === index) {
				updateDots(safe);
				animating = false;
				return;
			}
			const current = items[index];
			const nextItem = items[safe];
			const dir = direction >= 0 ? 1 : -1;
			nextItem.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
			nextItem.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
			requestAnimationFrame(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? '-translate-x-full' : 'translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			});
			updateDots(safe);
			setTimeout(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.add('hidden');
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove('translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
				index = safe;
				animating = false;
			}, transitionMs);
		};

		const stop = () => {
			if (!timer) return;
			clearTimeout(timer);
			timer = null;
		};
		const schedule = () => {
			stop();
			timer = setTimeout(() => go(1, { force: true }), intervalMs);
		};
		const go = (stepOrIndex, options = {}) => {
			const { absolute = false, force = false } = options;
			if (animating && !force) return;
			const nextIndex = absolute ? stepOrIndex : index + stepOrIndex;
			const direction = absolute ? (nextIndex > index ? 1 : -1) : stepOrIndex;
			show(nextIndex, direction);
			schedule();
		};

		items.forEach((item, i) => {
			if (i === index) {
				item.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			} else {
				item.classList.add('hidden');
				item.classList.remove('translate-x-0', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-full');
			}
		});
		updateDots(index);
		schedule();

		if (prev) {
			prev.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(-1);
			});
		}
		if (next) {
			next.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(1);
			});
		}

		dots.forEach((dot) => {
			dot.addEventListener('click', () => {
				const nextIndex = Number(dot.getAttribute('data-l7-slide-to') || 0);
				go(nextIndex, { absolute: true });
			});
		});

		let startX = 0;
		let startY = 0;
		let tracking = false;

		root.addEventListener('touchstart', (event) => {
			if (event.target && event.target.closest && event.target.closest('[data-l7-slide-to]')) {
				tracking = false;
				return;
			}
			if (!event.touches || event.touches.length !== 1) return;
			tracking = true;
			const touch = event.touches[0];
			startX = touch.clientX;
			startY = touch.clientY;
			stop();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchend', (event) => {
			if (!tracking) return;
			tracking = false;
			const touch = event.changedTouches && event.changedTouches[0];
			if (!touch) {
				schedule();
				return;
			}
			const dx = touch.clientX - startX;
			const dy = touch.clientY - startY;
			if (Math.abs(dx) > 40 && Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
				go(dx < 0 ? 1 : -1);
				return;
			}
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchcancel', () => {
			tracking = false;
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });
	})();
	</script>

	
</div>

        <div class="flex absolute bottom-3 left-1/2 z-30 -translate-x-1/2 items-center gap-1">
			<button type="button" class=" rounded-full shadow-lg" aria-label="Anterior" data-l7-prev>
				<img class="h-6 w-6" src="https://www.eltelegrafo.com.ec/images/sitio/arrow-left.svg" alt="Anterior">
			</button>
        	<button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="true" aria-label="Slide 1" data-l7-slide-to="0"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 2" data-l7-slide-to="1"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 3" data-l7-slide-to="2"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 4" data-l7-slide-to="3"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 5" data-l7-slide-to="4"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 6" data-l7-slide-to="5"></button><button type="button" class="w-3 h-3 rounded-full bg-gray-200 dark:bg-gray-800" aria-current="false" aria-label="Slide 7" data-l7-slide-to="6"></button>			<button type="button" class=" rounded-full shadow-lg" aria-label="Siguiente" data-l7-next>
				<img class="h-6 w-6" src="https://www.eltelegrafo.com.ec/images/sitio/arrow-right.svg" alt="Siguiente">
			</button>

	</div>

	<script>
	(function() {
		const root = document.getElementById('default-carousel-1553');
		if (!root) return;
		const items = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-item]'));
		const dots = Array.from(root.querySelectorAll('[data-l7-slide-to]'));
		const prev = root.querySelector('[data-l7-prev]');
		const next = root.querySelector('[data-l7-next]');
		if (!items.length) return;

		let index = dots.findIndex((dot) => dot.getAttribute('aria-current') === 'true');
		if (index < 0) index = 0;

		const transitionMs = 1200;
		const intervalMs = 15000;
		let timer = null;
		let animating = false;
		let showToken = 0;
		const updateDots = (activeIndex) => {
			dots.forEach((dot, i) => {
				const isActive = i === activeIndex;
				dot.setAttribute('aria-current', isActive ? 'true' : 'false');
				if (isActive) {
					dot.classList.remove('dot-animate');
					void dot.offsetWidth;
					dot.classList.add('dot-animate');
				}
			});
		};

		const show = (next, direction = 1) => {
			const total = items.length;
			const safe = ((next % total) + total) % total;
			showToken += 1;
			const token = showToken;
			animating = true;
			if (safe === index) {
				updateDots(safe);
				animating = false;
				return;
			}
			const current = items[index];
			const nextItem = items[safe];
			const dir = direction >= 0 ? 1 : -1;
			nextItem.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
			nextItem.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
			requestAnimationFrame(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? '-translate-x-full' : 'translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			});
			updateDots(safe);
			setTimeout(() => {
				if (token !== showToken) return;
				current.classList.add('hidden');
				current.classList.remove('translate-x-0', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				current.classList.add(dir > 0 ? 'translate-x-full' : '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.remove('translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				nextItem.classList.add('translate-x-0');
				index = safe;
				animating = false;
			}, transitionMs);
		};

		const stop = () => {
			if (!timer) return;
			clearTimeout(timer);
			timer = null;
		};
		const schedule = () => {
			stop();
			timer = setTimeout(() => go(1, { force: true }), intervalMs);
		};
		const go = (stepOrIndex, options = {}) => {
			const { absolute = false, force = false } = options;
			if (animating && !force) return;
			const next = absolute ? stepOrIndex : index + stepOrIndex;
			const direction = absolute ? (next > index ? 1 : -1) : stepOrIndex;
			show(next, direction);
			schedule();
		};

		items.forEach((item, i) => {
			if (i === index) {
				item.classList.remove('hidden', 'translate-x-full', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-0');
			} else {
				item.classList.add('hidden');
				item.classList.remove('translate-x-0', '-translate-x-full');
				item.classList.add('translate-x-full');
			}
		});
		updateDots(index);
		schedule();

		if (prev) {
			prev.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(-1);
			});
		}
		if (next) {
			next.addEventListener('click', () => {
				go(1);
			});
		}

		dots.forEach((dot) => {
			dot.addEventListener('click', () => {
				const next = Number(dot.getAttribute('data-l7-slide-to') || 0);
				go(next, { absolute: true });
			});
		});

		let startX = 0;
		let startY = 0;
		let tracking = false;

		root.addEventListener('touchstart', (event) => {
			if (event.target && event.target.closest && event.target.closest('[data-l7-slide-to]')) {
				tracking = false;
				return;
			}
			if (!event.touches || event.touches.length !== 1) return;
			tracking = true;
			const touch = event.touches[0];
			startX = touch.clientX;
			startY = touch.clientY;
			stop();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchend', (event) => {
			if (!tracking) return;
			tracking = false;
			const touch = event.changedTouches && event.changedTouches[0];
			if (!touch) {
				schedule();
				return;
			}
			const dx = touch.clientX - startX;
			const dy = touch.clientY - startY;
			if (Math.abs(dx) > 40 && Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
				go(dx < 0 ? 1 : -1);
				return;
			}
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });

		root.addEventListener('touchcancel', () => {
			tracking = false;
			schedule();
		}, { passive: true });
	})();
	</script>

	
</div>

  <path d="M4.19.01C.71.21-1.21,4.21.84,7.06c1.99,2.77,6.26,2.35,7.67-.75C9.9,3.25,7.53-.18,4.19.01ZM7.07,5.26H1.85v-1.61h5.22v1.61Z"/></svg></a></div></div></div></div></div><div class="sppb-col-sm-10 basis-full md:basis-13/16  "><div class="sppb-addon-container" style=""><div class="addon-module py-1"><div id="mod-1555" class="s-layout-6 s-mod style-d3c4e3 ">

		<article class="mx-auto w-full flex flex-wrap item s" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
			<div class="image basis-1/4 md:basis-full">
